SECURITY THE OBLIGATIONS OF THE BORROWER UNDER THE FACILITY AND ALL INTEREST AND OTHER MONIES IN RESPECT THEREOF, SUBJECT TO APPLICABLE LAWS SHALL BE SECURED BY EXCLUSIVE CHARGE, ON A POOL OF RECEIVABLES OF THE BORROWER SEGREGATED FOR ICIC BANK, AT LEAST EQUAL TO 1.10 TIMES THE OUTSTANDING FACILITY AMOUNT. IN CASE ANY OF THE ASSETS UNDER THE PORTFOLIO TURNS NPA, THE SAME SHALL BE REPLACED BY ASSET OF EQUIVALENT AMOUNT. (A)THE AGGREGATE VALUE OF THE SECURED ASSETS SHALL BE AT LEAST EQUAL TO 1.10 TIMES THE OUTSTANDING FACILITY AMOUNT ("SECURITY COVER") DURING THE CURRENCY OF THE FACILITY. (B)THE BORROWER SHALL SUBMIT STATEMENT OF RECEIVABLES FROM THE ASSET CREATED FROM ON-LENDING OF THE PROCEEDS OF THE FACILITY EVERY QUARTER STARTING FROM 90TH DAY FROM THE INITIAL DRAWDOWN DATE. THE CALCULATION OF THE QUARTER WILL BE FROM INITIAL DRAWDOWN DATE. THE SECURITY MENTIONED ABOVE SHALL BE CREATED / FURNISHED IN FAVOUR OF LENDER IN A FORM AND MANNER ACCEPTABLE TO LENDER SECURITY COVER THE AGGREGATE VALUE OF THE SECURED ASSETS SHALL BE AT LEAST EQUAL TO 1.10 TIMES THE OUTSTANDING FACILITY AMOUNT "SECURITY COVER") DURING THE CURRENCY OF THE FACILITY. HEDGING CLAUSE IN CASE THE BORROWER DECIDES TO AVAIL FOREIGN CURRENCY FACILITIES IN FUTURE IT WILL COMPLY WITH FOLLOWING TERMS (I) THE BOARD OF DIRECTORS OF THE BORROWER HAS APPROVED RISK MANAGEMENT POLICY, IN LINE WITH RELEVANT RBI CIRCULARS, TO BE ADOPTED BY THE BORROWER, WHICH INCLUDES, AMONG OTHER THINGS, THE RISK LIMITS FOR VARIOUS RISK EXPOSURES AND MECHANISMS TO ADDRESS THE IMPACT OF FOREX RATE VOLATILITY ON THE BORROWER'S ABILITY TO CONDUCT ITS BUSINESS AND SERVICE ITS DEBT. THE BOARD CLOSELY MONITORS CHANGING MARKET CONDITIONS AND REGULATORY CHANGES BEING ANNOUNCED, INCLUDING THOSE RELATING TO CROSS BORDER TRANSACTIONS WHETHER WITH GROUP COMPANIES OR OTHERWISE; AND B.
